<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 2.02&nbsp;Results of Operations and
Financial Condition.</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On January 24,
2007, the Registrant issued a press release and held a conference call with
analysts to report on the results of operations for the fourth quarter of
fiscal year 2006, which ended on November 30, 2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Furnished with
this Form&nbsp;8-K as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 is a copy of the press release labeled &#147;McCormick
Reports Excellent Results for 2006 Fourth Quarter and Fiscal Year; Expects
Strong Growth in 2007,&#148; which includes a Consolidated Income Statement for the
three and twelve month periods ended November 30, 2006 and November 30, 2005, a
Consolidated Balance Sheet of the Registrant as of November 30, 2006 and
November 30, 2005, and an Consolidated Statement of Cash Flows for the twelve
months ended November 30, 2006 and November 30, 2005.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 9.01 Financial
Statements and Exhibits.</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)&#160; Exhibits.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The exhibit to
this report is listed in Item 2.02 above and in the Exhibit Index that follows
the signature line.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">SIGNATURES</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 24.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pursuant to the requirements of the Securities
Exchange Act of 1934, the Registrant has duly caused this report to be signed
on its behalf by the undersigned hereunto duly authorized.</font></p>

<div>


<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit
99.1</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><img width="604" height="93" src="g23491mm01i001.jpg"></font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:324.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">FOR IMMEDIATE
RELEASE</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">McCORMICK REPORTS EXCELLENT RESULTS
FOR 2006 FOURTH QUARTER AND FISCAL YEAR; EXPECTS STRONG GROWTH IN 2007</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">SPARKS,
MD, JANUARY 24 - - - McCormick &amp; Company, Incorporated (NYSE:MKC), today
reported results for the fourth quarter and fiscal year ended November 30,
2006.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b>Increased sales 5% during 2006.&#160;
Higher volume from new products, marketing programs and ethnic flavors
including a 2006 acquisition, as well as pricing actions, drove this increase.</b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b>Achieved a 1.0 percentage point increase in gross profit margin,
reaching 41.0% for the year.</b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b>Reported earnings per share of $1.50 compared to $1.56 in 2005.&#160; However, on a comparable basis, excluding
restructuring charges and stock-based compensation expense, earnings per share
increased significantly in 2006.</b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b>For fiscal year 2007, expect to grow sales 4-6% and increase earnings
per share 8-10% on a comparable basis.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Robert
J. Lawless, Chairman and CEO, commented, &#147;Our financial performance in 2006
exceeded our expectations.&#160; We had four
quarters of excellent financial results with strong contributions from both the
consumer and industrial businesses.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;This
was achieved during a time of significant change at the Company.&#160; A restructuring plan that is underway
included the consolidation of several large facilities.&#160; In the U.S., we began the transformation of
our industrial business and in the consumer business we embarked on a
significant revitalization program for our spice and seasoning line.&#160; In Europe we successfully implemented SAP and
increased sales of core herbs and spices in the U.K. and France.&#160; Each of these major initiatives was
well-planned and well-executed.&#160; In
addition, we acquired a promising new business in the U.S., Simply Asia Foods,
which established a leadership position for McCormick in the Thai foods
category.&#160; Never have I seen so much
accomplished so quickly.&#160; The foundation
of our success is the leadership, hard work and talent of McCormick employees
around the world.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Our
business continues to generate a high level of cash from operations.&#160; Cash was used in 2006 to fund an acquisition,
pay dividends, repurchase shares and fund capital projects that improved
productivity.&#160; Of cash from operations,
81% was returned to shareholders in the form of dividends and share
repurchases.&#160; In November we announced an
11% increase in the quarterly dividend per share.&#148;</font></p>


<br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\fc\2318385485_D11624_1631814\2349-1-mm-01.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Jan 23 18:38 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Fiscal
year results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the fiscal year, the Company increased sales 5%.&#160; A number of products led to higher sales
volume including convenience items, new flavor varieties for grilling, lower
salt alternatives and products with ethnic flavors.&#160; The Company continued to increase marketing
support in both North America and Europe, with advertising expenditures up more
than 25% in 2006.&#160; The portfolio of U.S.
consumer products was expanded with the acquisition of the Simply Asia Foods
business during the year.&#160; Also
positively impacting sales were pricing actions taken early in 2006 in response
to higher costs of certain materials, employee benefits and energy.&#160; The impact of foreign currency was minimal
for the fiscal year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Gross
profit margin reached 41.0%, a significant increase from 40.0% in the prior
year.&#160; Gross profit margin was net of
restructuring charges, which reduced the margin by 0.5 percentage points. The
increase in margin was driven by our initiatives to reduce costs, pricing
actions and a more favorable product mix.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Earnings
per share were $1.50 compared to $1.56 in 2005.&#160;
Charges related to the Company&#146;s restructuring program reduced earnings
per share 22&#162; in 2006 and 5&#162; in 2005.&#160;
Stock-based compensation expense, which the Company began to record in
the first quarter of 2006, reduced earnings per share 11&#162;.&#160; During the year, higher sales and gross
profit margin, net of an increase in operating expenses, added 10&#162; to earnings
per share.&#160; The increase in operating
expenses included higher advertising support and incentive compensation.&#160; Earnings per share were further increased by
a lower tax rate which added 6&#162;, a 2% reduction in diluted shares outstanding
which added 4&#162;, and increases in other income and income from unconsolidated
operations which added 2&#162;.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During
2006, significant cash from operations was generated, totaling $311
million.&#160; Mid-year, the Company increased
its debt level to fund a portion of the acquisition of Simply Asia Foods. For
the fiscal year, the primary uses of cash were $156 million for share
repurchases, $103 million for acquisitions, $95 million for dividends and $79
million for net capital expenditures.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Fourth quarter
results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the fourth quarter, the Company increased sales 9%, a 7% increase in local
currency.&#160; As in the fiscal year, this
growth was due to volume gains with new products, effective marketing and the
addition of Simply Asia Foods, as well as pricing actions.&#160; In the fourth quarter, the Company nearly
doubled advertising to drive sales during the important holiday season and into
2007 for markets in North America and Europe.&#160;
The fourth quarter sales increase was net of the effects of our ongoing
strategy to reduce low margin business, which reduced sales approximately 1%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Gross
profit margin reached 44.3% compared to 43.9% in the prior year.&#160; Gross profit margin was net of restructuring
charges, which reduced the margin by 0.6 percentage points.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Earnings
per share were 62&#162; compared to 65&#162; in 2005.&#160;
Charges related to the Company&#146;s restructuring program reduced earnings
per share 10&#162; in the fourth quarter of 2006 and 5&#162; in the fourth quarter of
2005.&#160; Stock-based compensation expense,
which the Company began to record in the first quarter of 2006, reduced
earnings per share 2&#162;.&#160; During the
quarter, higher sales and improved gross profit margin more than offset a
significant increase in advertising and higher incentive compensation
expense.&#160; Earnings per share increased 3&#162;
from</font></p>


<br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\fc\2318385485_D11624_1631814\2349-1-mm-01.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Jan 23 18:38 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">a lower tax rate,
decreased 2&#162; due to lower income from unconsolidated operations and increased
1&#162; from a reduction in diluted shares outstanding.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Financial
outlook</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Mr. Lawless further stated, &#147;There is great momentum
as we begin 2007 and we expect another year of excellent financial
results.&#160; The restructuring program
announced at the end of 2005 will generate significant savings in 2007.&#160; We met our cost reduction target of $10
million in 2006 and project cost savings of $30 million in 2007.&#160; We are particularly excited about the roll
out of our revitalization program for our consumer spice and seasoning line in
the U.S.&#160; The increased sales for this part
of our business in the second half of 2006 are an early sign of success with
this initiative together with increased advertising.&#160; For our industrial business, operating profit
margins will continue to benefit from our transformation actions in the U.S.
and additional efforts in international markets.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company expects to increase 2007 earnings per
share in the 8-10% range on a comparable basis with 2006 which excludes
restructuring charges.&#160; Sales are
expected to grow 4-6% with a full year impact of Simply Asia, the continued
roll out of the spice and seasoning revitalization program in the U.S., and
further success with new product introductions and other growth
initiatives.&#160; This sales increase is net
of reductions from the elimination of lower margin products, which will
continue into 2007.&#160; Gross profit margin
is projected to increase approximately 0.5 percentage points, on a comparable
basis with 2006, excluding restructuring charges.&#160; Including estimated restructuring charges of
18&#162;, earnings per share for 2007 are projected to be in the range of
$1.67-$1.71.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Business
Segment Results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">In the
first quarter of 2006, the Company made several changes to the way it reports
its business segment results.&#160; These
changes are described following the financial results for the consumer and
industrial businesses.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Consumer
Business</font></b></p>

<p style="line-height:1.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><hr size="1" width="160" noshade color="black" align="left" style="width:120.0pt;"></div>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">*&#160;
The Company began recording stock-based compensation expense in the
first quarter of 2006.&#160; Stock
compensation expense recorded in the consumer business operating results was $2.2
million in the fourth quarter and $13.9 million year-to-date.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the fiscal year, sales for McCormick&#146;s consumer business rose 5% compared to
2005, with no significant impact from foreign currency.&#160; The Company drove sales with higher volume
from successful new products and effective marketing programs, the acquisition
of Simply Asia Foods and pricing actions.&#160;
Consumer sales in the Americas rose 8% due to higher volume from new
products, brand support, including increased advertising support, and the
acquisition of Simply Asia Foods, as well as pricing.&#160; Foreign exchange rates had a positive impact
of less than 1% in this region.&#160; In
Europe, consumer sales declined 1%, but in local currency rose 1%.&#160; Increased sales of core spices and herbs in
both the U.K. and France were offset in part by distribution lost to a
competitor in The Netherlands early in the year, as well as</font></p>


<br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\fc\2318385485_D11624_1631814\2349-1-mm-01.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Jan 23 18:38 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">the Company&#146;s
decision to exit its business in Finland.&#160;
In the Asia/Pacific region, the Company increased sales 1%, and in local
currency, 2%.&#160; Sales in China rose 14% in
local currency, while Australia was affected by discontinued sales of a lower
margin product line.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the consumer business, fiscal year 2006 operating income, excluding
restructuring charges, was $278 million compared to $288 million in 2005.&#160; This includes $14 million of stock-based
compensation expense recorded in 2006.&#160;
An increase of $17 million was driven by higher sales and gross profit
margin, partially offset by higher incentive compensation.&#160; In addition, the Company increased advertising
expenditures $13 million to support the sale of its brands in domestic and
international markets.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the fourth quarter, similar factors affected consumer sales in each
region.&#160; In total, consumer sales rose
10% compared to the prior year, and in local currency increased 8%.&#160; Sales in the Americas rose 11% with a minimal
impact from foreign exchange rates.&#160;
Consumer sales in Europe rose 6%, but in local currency were unchanged
from 2005.&#160; In the Asia/Pacific region,
the Company increased sales 1%, and in local currency, sales were even with
last year.&#160; Fourth quarter operating
income excluding restructuring charges was $122 million compared to $125
million in 2005.&#160; This included the
negative impact of $2 million of stock-based compensation expense recorded in
2006.&#160; An increase of $8 million was
driven by higher sales and gross profit margin, net of higher incentive
compensation.&#160; In addition, the Company
increased advertising expenditures $9 million in the fourth quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Industrial
Business</font></b></p>

<p style="line-height:1.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><hr size="1" width="160" noshade color="black" align="left" style="width:120.0pt;"></div>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">*&#160;
The Company began recording stock-based compensation expense in the
first quarter of 2006.&#160; Stock
compensation expense recorded in the industrial business operating results was
$1.6 million in the fourth quarter and $8.1 million year-to-date.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the fiscal year, sales for McCormick&#146;s industrial business increased 4%
compared to the prior year, with no significant impact from foreign exchange
rates.&#160; The increase was driven primarily
by higher volume related to new product introductions.&#160; The elimination of low margin business
reduced sales 1% during the year.&#160; In the
Americas, industrial sales rose 5%, and in local currency 4%.&#160; This increase was achieved despite the
elimination of low margin business which reduced sales 1%.&#160;&#160; Sales of new products to strategic customers
were the primary driver of higher sales in this region.&#160; In Europe, the Company increased sales 4%,
and in local currency 5% with increases in snack seasonings and products sold
to quick service restaurants.&#160; These
sales increases were achieved despite a<i></i>1% reduction
due to the elimination of low margin business.&#160;
Sales in the Asia/Pacific region decreased 2%, and in local currency
decreased 4%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the industrial business, fiscal year operating income, excluding restructuring
charges, was $76 million compared to $67 million in 2005.&#160; This included an $8 million negative impact
of stock-based compensation expense recorded in 2006.&#160; A significant increase of $17 million was
driven by higher sales and gross profit margin during the year, partially
offset by increased incentive compensation.&#160;
Cost savings from the Company&#146;s restructuring plan and a</font></p>


<br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\fc\2318385485_D11624_1631814\2349-1-mm-01.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Jan 23 18:38 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">focus on strategic
customers lifted margins in 2006.&#160; Also,
the industrial business was negatively impacted in 2005 by several factors
including extreme volatility in the vanilla market.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the fourth quarter, similar factors affected industrial sales in each
region.&#160; In total, industrial sales rose
8% compared to the prior year, and in local currency increased 6%.&#160; The elimination of low margin business
reduced sales 1% during this period.&#160;
Sales in the Americas rose 3% with minimal impact from foreign currency
rates.&#160;&#160; During the fourth quarter, the
elimination of low margin business reduced sales 2% in this region.&#160; Industrial sales in Europe rose 27%, and in
local currency 21%, due to increased sales of seasonings for chicken,
condiments and other food service products.&#160;&#160;
In the Asia/Pacific region, the Company increased sales 9%, and in local
currency 6%.&#160; Fourth quarter operating
income excluding restructuring charges was $23 million compared to $21 million
in 2005.&#160; This includes $2 million of
stock-based compensation expense in 2006.&#160;
Higher sales and gross profit margin, net of increased incentive
compensation, contributed $4 million to operating income during this period.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Changes
in Reporting Business Segment Results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In
the first quarter of 2006, the Company changed the way it internally reports
its business segment results.&#160; In line
with this change, the segment results above have also been changed and prior
periods have been restated to be comparable.&#160;
The changes are summarized below:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Operating
income internally is measured by management excluding restructuring
charges.&#160; The information provided above displays
operating income for each segment with and without restructuring charges.&#160; As noted below, management believes this
information is relevant to analyze business performance and trends.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
Company decided to allocate 100% of its selling, general and administrative
expenses to the business segments beginning in the first quarter of 2006. The
Company believes that this more complete allocation better represents the
profitability of its two segments.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
sales and income related to warehouse club customers are now managed in the
consumer business.&#160; Through 2005, this
was managed in the industrial business.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Company has posted to its website, restated historical business segment results
for each quarter of 2005 at ir.mccormick.com under the heading &#147;Financial
Information&#148; and &#147;2005 Business Segment Restatement.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In
addition to the changes noted above, the Company also adopted SFAS 123R, which
resulted in the Company recording stock-based compensation expense beginning in
the first quarter of 2006. This has a significant effect on each of the
business segments and accordingly, the effect is noted with the segment
financial results reported above.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Non-GAAP
Financial Measures</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The pro forma information excluding restructuring
charges in this press release are not measures that are defined in generally
accepted accounting principles (&#147;GAAP&#148;).&#160;
These items are measures that management believes are important to
adjust for in order to have a meaningful comparison to prior and future periods
and to provide a basis for future projections and for estimating our earnings
growth prospects.&#160; These non-GAAP
measures are used by</font></p>


<br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\fc\2318385485_D11624_1631814\2349-1-mm-01.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Jan 23 18:38 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">management as a performance measure to judge profitability of our
business absent the restructuring related items.&#160; Management analyzes the Company&#146;s business
performance and trends excluding amounts related to the restructuring.&#160; These measures provide a more consistent view
of performance than the closest GAAP equivalent for management and investors.&#160; Management compensates for this by using
these measures in combination with the GAAP measures.&#160; The presentation of the non-GAAP measures in
this press release are made alongside the most directly comparable GAAP
measures.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Pro
forma Information</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Company has provided below certain pro forma financial results excluding
amounts related to its restructuring programs.&#160;
In addition, the impact of stock-based compensation expense, which the
Company began to record in &#147;Selling, general and administrative expense&#148; in the
first quarter of 2006, is noted.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:1.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">No stock-based
compensation expense was recorded in 2005.&#160;
In the fourth quarter of 2006, stock-based compensation expense of $3.8
million had an after-tax impact of $2.7 million.&#160; For the fiscal year, stock-based compensation
expense of $22.0 million had an after-tax impact of $15.1 million.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">No stock-based
compensation expense was recorded in 2005.&#160;
In the fourth quarter of 2006, stock-based compensation expense reduced
earnings per share by $0.02.&#160; For the
fiscal year, stock-based compensation expense reduced earnings per share by
$0.11.&#160; On a comparable basis, excluding
both restructuring charges and stock-based compensation expense, fiscal year
2006 diluted earnings per share rose 13.7%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About
McCormick</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">McCormick
&amp; Company, Incorporated is the global leader in the manufacture, marketing
and distribution of spices, seasonings and flavors to the entire food industry &#150;
to foodservice and food manufacturers as well as to retail outlets.</font></p>

Quarter Report&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; McCormick
&amp; Company, Incorporated</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Consolidated Cash Flow Statement</font></b></p>
